Each level builds on increasing responsibility, technical expertise, and leadership within the Operational Technology (OT) cybersecurity program. Analysts are responsible for protecting, maintaining, and continuously improving the security of OT environments, ensuring compliance with regulatory and industry standards such as NERC CIP and NIST. Level 1 – Cyber Security Analyst Position Concept: The Level 1 Cyber Security Analyst supports OT cybersecurity maintenance activities, manages cyber asset inventories, assists in the implementation of cybersecurity programs, and ensures security controls are applied consistently across operational systems. Key Responsibilities: Identify and document OT cyber assets; extract and update asset configurations in the database. Install security patches, update antivirus definitions, and perform system backups. Maintain baselines of operational systems; update cybersecurity SharePoint sites for stakeholder engagement. Monitor CVE releases and assess applicability to OT assets. Provide IT-related support for OT systems (e.g., HMIs, network appliances, remote connectivity). Required Knowledge/Skills/Abilities: Basic understanding of industrial automation systems (ABB, Allen Bradley, Emerson, etc.) or operating system security (Windows, Linux/Unix, Mac OS). Familiarity with endpoint, server, and network security tools such as Firewalls, IDS/IPS, SIEM, Antivirus, and DLP. Knowledge of forensic investigation techniques for logs, networks, and systems. Working knowledge of networking protocols and system administration. Ability to recognize and investigate indicators of compromise. Strong analytical, communication, and risk assessment skills. Preferred Skills: Experience applying patches, antivirus updates, and performing backups. Experience troubleshooting network communications. Supporting compliance audits. Designing/implementing industrial automation or network architecture. Level 2 – Senior Cyber Security Analyst Position Concept: The Level 2 Analyst is responsible for assessing OT vulnerabilities, ensuring secure configurations, and developing remediation plans. The role includes mentoring junior analysts, developing cybersecurity maintenance procedures, and providing guidance for program compliance. Key Responsibilities: Evaluate OT network architecture, system configurations, and external connections for compliance. Review vendor manuals, training materials, and industry standards to develop cybersecurity procedures. Mentor and provide guidance to Level 1 Analysts. Monitor and assess new CVEs for applicability to OT systems. Support incident response, security intelligence monitoring, and OT awareness initiatives. Required Knowledge/Skills/Abilities: Advanced knowledge of OS security (Windows, Linux/Unix, Mac OS), web servers, and network security. Hands-on experience with security tools: Firewalls, IDS/IPS, SIEM, Endpoint Security, File Integrity Monitoring, etc. Proficiency in forensic investigation (logs, networks, systems). Strong knowledge of scripting (Python, Bash, PowerShell). Familiarity with penetration testing tools and techniques. Understanding of compliance frameworks (NERC CIP, SOX, PCI). Strong communication, risk assessment, and analytical skills. Level 3 – Lead Cyber Security Analyst Position Concept: The Lead Analyst is responsible for maintaining and improving OT cybersecurity frameworks, overseeing compliance activities, leading vulnerability management efforts, and ensuring alignment with industry standards. This role leads cross-departmental collaboration, trains staff and provides subject matter expertise for audits and regulatory engagements. Key Responsibilities: Translate standards (NERC CIP, NIST CSF, NIST 800-53) into systemic and procedural solutions. Maintain and improve OT cybersecurity standards, procedures, and maintenance schedules. Lead vulnerability management and remediation programs. Evaluate OT systems for compliance with regulatory and internal standards. Develop management responses for internal/external audits. Facilitate IT/OT collaboration and train staff on cybersecurity best practices. Required Knowledge/Skills/Abilities: Expertise in developing and implementing OT cybersecurity programs. Strong knowledge of OS, web, and network security across enterprise and OT environments. Advanced expertise in security tools (Firewalls, IDS/IPS, SIEM, DLP, Endpoint Security, etc.). Deep knowledge of forensic investigation, malware analysis, and packet analysis. Proficiency in scripting (Python, Bash, PowerShell). Strong knowledge of compliance frameworks (NERC CIP, SOX, PCI). style=\"mso-special-character:line-break\">\r\n<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">Job Overview:</span></b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\"><o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">VDOT is seeking an experienced Senior Security\r\nOperations Engineer with in-depth knowledge and hands on experience in the\r\nareas of Information Systems security, security policy, intrusion\r\ndetection/prevention systems, firewalls, anti-virus software, anti-malware,\r\nanti-phishing, authentication systems, log analysis and management, web content\r\nfiltering; network protocols and security/authentication protocols at all\r\nlayers of the OSI model with emphasis on TCP/IP, web security gateways, network\r\naccess control, endpoint security, and perimeter security technologies. The\r\nSenior Security Operations Engineer contributes to the overall technology\r\nroadmap.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">Key Responsibilities:</span></b><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\"><o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">•<span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Participates\r\nin the design, implementation and support of security infrastructure for the\r\nDepartment.&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">•<span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Identifies\r\nnetwork and information security risks across the enterprise, design, engineer,\r\nimplement security solutions to address the risks at an enterprise level.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">•<span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Works\r\nclosely with the IT Division and outside vendors to effectively design, plan,\r\ndeploy, secure and update network projects in the environment.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">•<span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Effective\r\ncollaboration with the Office of Information Security OIS and other ITD groups\r\nis maintained.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">•<span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Strategic\r\nPlan items pertinent to the Network Security Operations group are completed.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">•<span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>System\r\npolicies and procedures are created, documented, and maintained.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">•<span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Perform\r\nnetwork scans and penetration testing. Monitors log analysis and management\r\ntools for threats.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">•<span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Evaluate\r\nvulnerability scan results and notify business, application, and infrastructure\r\nteams of vulnerabilities in need of remediation.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">•<span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Evaluate\r\nand participate in agency Azure cloud solution review of network, security, and\r\ngeneral project involvement.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">•<span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Ensure\r\nall daily functions that are required to maintain security applicable systems\r\nand applications are documented.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">•<span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Work\r\nwith the agency’s ISO team and the IT Auditors to review security audit\r\nfindings and vulnerability scans results.&nbsp; Identify recommended correction\r\nactivities and course of action, once determined communicate with the various\r\nstakeholders.<o:p></o:p></span></p>\r\n\r\n<p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;line-height:normal\"><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt\">•<span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
